When the hell did people start calling thumbsticks on a controller "joysticks"?  A joystick is a long, "stick"-shaped device that has buttons on it and can move on an analogue, spherical axis. Thumbsticks have this same movement, but they're much smaller and lack personal buttons, instead being additions to a larger controller.
